lark-cli","","[![License: MIT](https://img.shields.io/badge/License-MIT-yellow.svg)](https://opensource.org/licenses/MIT)","[![Go Version](https://img.shields.io/badge/go-%3E%3D1.23-blue.svg)](https://go.dev/)","[![npm version](https://img.shields.io/npm/v/@larksuite/cli.svg)](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@larksuite/cli)","","[中文版](./README.zh.md) | [English](./README.md)","","The official [Lark/Feishu](https://www.larksuite.com/) CLI tool, maintained by the [larksuite](https://github.com/larksuite) team — built for humans and AI Agents. Covers core business domains including Messenger, Docs, Base, Sheets, Slides, Calendar, Mail, Tasks, Meetings, Markdown, and more, with 200+ commands and 26 AI Agent [Skills](./skills/).","","[Install](#installation--quick-start) · [AI Agent Skills](#agent-skills) · [Auth](#authentication) · [Commands](#three-layer-command-system) · [Advanced](#advanced-usage) · [Security](#security--risk-warnings-read-before-use) · [Contributing](#contributing)","","## Why lark-cli?","","- **Agent-Native Design** — 24 structured [Skills](./skills/) out of the box, compatible with popular AI tools — Agents can operate Lark with zero extra setup","- **Wide Coverage** — 18 business domains, 200+ curated commands, 26 AI Agent [Skills](./skills/)","- **AI-Friendly \u0026 Optimized** — Every command is tested with real Agents, featuring concise parameters, smart defaults, and structured output to maximize Agent call success rates","- **Open Source, Zero Barriers** — MIT license, ready to use, just `npm install`","- **Up and Running in 3 Minutes** — One-click app creation, interactive login, from install to first API call in just 3 steps","- **Secure \u0026 Controllable** — Input injection protection, terminal output sanitization, OS-native keychain credential storage","- **Three-Layer Architecture** — Shortcuts (human \u0026 AI friendly) → API Commands (platform-synced) → Raw API (full coverage), choose the right granularity","","## Features","","| Category      | Capabilities                                                                                                                      |","| ------------- |-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|","| 📅 Calendar   | View, create and update events, invite attendees, find meeting rooms, RSVP to invitations, check free/busy \u0026 time suggestions     |","| 💬 Messenger  | Send/reply messages, create and manage group chats, view chat history \u0026 threads, search messages, download media                  |","| 📄 Docs       | Create, read, update, and search documents, read/write media \u0026 whiteboards                                                        |","| 📁 Drive      | Upload and download files, search docs \u0026 wiki, manage comments                                                                    |","| 📝 Markdown   | Create, fetch, patch, and overwrite Drive-native `.md` files                                                                      |","| 📊 Base       | Create and manage tables, fields, records, views, dashboards, workflows, forms, roles \u0026 permissions, data aggregation \u0026 analytics |","| 📈 Sheets     | Create, read, write, append, find, and export spreadsheet data                                                                    |","| 🖼️ Slides     | Create and manage presentations, read presentation content, and add or remove slides                                              |","| ✅ Tasks      | Create, query, update, and complete tasks; manage task lists, subtasks, comments \u0026 reminders                                      |","| 📚 Wiki       | Create and manage knowledge spaces, nodes, and documents                                                                          |","| 👤 Contact    | Search users by name/email/phone, get user profiles                                                                               |","| 📧 Mail       | Browse, search, read emails, send, reply, forward, manage drafts, watch new mail                                                  |","| 🎥 Meetings   | Search meeting records, query meeting minutes artifacts and recordings                                                            |","| 🕐 Attendance | Query personal attendance check-in records                                                                                        |","| ✍️ Approval   | Query approval tasks, approve/reject/transfer tasks, cancel and CC instances                                                      |","| 🎯 OKR        | Query, create, update OKRs; manage objective \u0026 key results, alignments, indicators and progress.                                  |","| 📋 Project    | Meegle — manage work items, schedules, and data via the standalone [meegle-cli](https://github.com/larksuite/meegle-cli) (install separately) |","| 🔗 Apps       | Create Spark/Miaoda apps, publish HTML/static sites, run cloud generation, and manage access scope                                 |","","## Installation \u0026 Quick Start","","### Requirements","","Before you start, make sure you have:","","- Node.js (`npm`/`npx`)","- Go `v1.23`+ and Python 3 (only required for building from source)","","### Quick Start (Human Users)","","\u003e **Note for AI assistants:** If you are an AI Agent helping the user with installation, jump directly to [Quick Start (AI Agent)](#quick-start-ai-agent), which contains all the steps you need to complete.","","#### Install","","Choose **one** of the following methods:","","**Option 1 — From npm (recommended):**","","```bash","npx @larksuite/cli@latest install","```","","**Option 2 — From source:**","","Requires Go `v1.23`+ and Python 3.","","```bash","git clone https://github.com/larksuite/cli.git","cd cli","make install","","# Install CLI SKILL (required)","npx skills add larksuite/cli -y -g","```","","#### Configure \u0026 Use","","```bash","# 1. Configure app credentials (one-time, interactive guided setup)","lark-cli config init","","# 2. Log in (--recommend auto-selects commonly used scopes)","lark-cli auth login --recommend","","# 3. Start using","lark-cli calendar +agenda","```","","## Quick Start (AI Agent)","","\u003e The following steps are for AI Agents. Some steps require the user to complete actions in a browser.","","**Step 1 — Install**","","```bash","npx @larksuite/cli@latest install","```","","**Step 2 — Configure app credentials**","","\u003e Run this command in the background. It will output an authorization URL — extract it and send it to the user. The command exits automatically after the user completes the setup in the browser.","","```bash","lark-cli config init --new","```","","**Step 3 — Login**","","\u003e Same as above: run in the background, extract the authorization URL and send it to the user.","","```bash","lark-cli auth login --recommend","```","","**Step 4 — Verify**","","```bash","lark-cli auth status","```","","## Agent Skills","","| Skill                           | Description                                                                                                    |","| ------------------------------- |----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|","| `lark-shared`                   | App config, auth login, identity switching, scope management, security rules (auto-loaded by all other skills) |","| `lark-calendar`                 | Calendar events (create/update), agenda view, free/busy queries, time suggestions, room finding, RSVP replies  |","| `lark-im`                       | Send/reply messages, group chat management, message search, upload/download images \u0026 files, reactions          |","| `lark-doc`                      | Create, read, update, search documents (Markdown-based)                                                        |","| `lark-drive`                    | Upload, download files, manage permissions \u0026 comments                                                          |","| `lark-markdown`                 | Create, fetch, patch, and overwrite Drive-native Markdown files                                                |","| `lark-sheets`                   | Create, read, write, append, find, export spreadsheets                                                         |","| `lark-slides`                   | Create and manage presentations, read presentation content, and add or remove slides                          |","| `lark-base`                     | Tables, fields, records, views, dashboards, data aggregation \u0026 analytics                                       |","| `lark-task`                     | Tasks, task lists, subtasks, reminders, member assignment                                                      |","| `lark-mail`                     | Browse, search, read emails, send, reply, forward, draft management, watch new mail                            |","| `lark-contact`                  | Search users by name/email/phone, get user profiles                                                            |","| `lark-wiki`                     | Knowledge spaces, nodes, documents                                                                             |","| `lark-event`                    | Real-time event subscriptions (WebSocket), regex routing \u0026 agent-friendly format                               |","| `lark-vc`                       | Search meeting records, query meeting minutes (summary, todos, transcript)                                     |","| `lark-whiteboard`               | Whiteboard/chart DSL rendering                                                                                 |","| `lark-minutes`                  | Minutes metadata \u0026 AI artifacts (summary, todos, chapters); upload audio/video to create minutes, download media |","| `lark-openapi-explorer`         | Explore underlying APIs from official docs                                                                     |","| `lark-skill-maker`              | Custom skill creation framework                                                                                |","| `lark-attendance`               | Query personal attendance check-in records                                                                     |","| `lark-approval`                 | Query approval tasks, approve/reject/transfer tasks, cancel and CC instances                                   |","| `lark-workflow-meeting-summary` | Workflow: meeting minutes aggregation \u0026 structured report                                                      |","| `lark-workflow-standup-report`  | Workflow: agenda \u0026 todo summary                                                                                |","| `lark-okr`                      | Query, create, update OKRs; manage objective \u0026 key results, alignments and indicators.                         |","","## Authentication","","| Command       | Description                                                    |","| ------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------- |","| `auth login`  | OAuth login with interactive selection or CLI flags for scopes |","| `auth logout` | Sign out and remove stored credentials                         |","| `auth status` | Show current login status and granted scopes                   |","| `auth check`  | Verify a specific scope (exit 0 = ok, 1 = missing)            |","| `auth scopes` | List all available scopes for the app                          |","| `auth list`   | List all authenticated users                                   |","","```bash","# Interactive login (TUI guides domain and permission level selection)","lark-cli auth login","","# Filter by domain","lark-cli auth login --domain calendar,task","","# Recommended auto-approval scopes","lark-cli auth login --recommend","","# Exact scope","lark-cli auth login --scope \"calendar:calendar:read\"","","# Agent mode: return verification URL immediately, non-blocking","lark-cli auth login --domain calendar --no-wait","# Resume polling later","lark-cli auth login --device-code \u003cDEVICE_CODE\u003e","","# Identity switching: execute commands as user or bot","lark-cli calendar +agenda --as user","lark-cli im +messages-send --as bot --chat-id \"oc_xxx\" --text \"Hello\"","```","","## Three-Layer Command System","","The CLI provides three levels of granularity, covering everything from quick operations to fully custom API calls:","","### 1. Shortcuts","","Prefixed with `+`, designed to be friendly for both humans and AI, with smart defaults, table output, and dry-run previews.","","```bash","lark-cli calendar +agenda","lark-cli im +messages-send --chat-id \"oc_xxx\" --text \"Hello\"","lark-cli docs +create --api-version v2 --doc-format markdown --content $'\u003ctitle\u003eWeekly Report\u003c/title\u003e\\n# Progress\\n- Completed feature X'","```","","Run `lark-cli \u003cservice\u003e --help` to see all shortcut commands.","","### 2. API Commands","","Auto-generated from Lark OAPI metadata, curated through evaluation and quality gates — 100+ commands mapped 1:1 to platform endpoints.","","```bash","lark-cli calendar calendars list","lark-cli calendar events instance_view --params '{\"calendar_id\":\"primary\",\"start_time\":\"1700000000\",\"end_time\":\"1700086400\"}'","```","","### 3. Raw API Calls","","Call any Lark Open Platform endpoint directly, covering 2500+ APIs.","","```bash","lark-cli api GET /open-apis/calendar/v4/calendars","lark-cli api POST /open-apis/im/v1/messages --params '{\"receive_id_type\":\"chat_id\"}' --data '{\"receive_id\":\"oc_xxx\",\"msg_type\":\"text\",\"content\":\"{\\\"text\\\":\\\"Hello\\\"}\"}'","```","","## Advanced Usage","","### Output Formats","","```bash","--format json      # Full JSON response (default)","--format pretty    # Human-friendly formatted output","--format table     # Readable table","--format ndjson    # Newline-delimited JSON (for piping)","--format csv       # Comma-separated values","```","","### Pagination","","```bash","--page-all                  # Auto-paginate through all pages","--page-limit 5              # Max 5 pages","--page-delay 500            # 500ms between page requests","```","","### Dry Run","","For commands that may have side effects, preview the request with --dry-run first:","","```bash","lark-cli im +messages-send --chat-id oc_xxx --text \"hello\" --dry-run","```","","### Schema Introspection","","Use schema to inspect any API method's parameters, request body, response structure, supported identities, and scopes:","","```bash","lark-cli schema","lark-cli schema calendar.events.instance_view","lark-cli schema im.messages.delete","```","","## Security \u0026 Risk Warnings (Read Before Use)","","This tool can be invoked by AI Agents to automate operations on the Lark/Feishu Open Platform, and carries inherent risks such as model hallucinations, unpredictable execution, and prompt injection. After you authorize Lark/Feishu permissions, the AI Agent will act under your user identity within the authorized scope, which may lead to high-risk consequences such as leakage of sensitive data or unauthorized operations. Please use with caution.","","To reduce these risks, the tool enables default security protections at multiple layers. However, these risks still exist. We strongly recommend that you do not proactively modify any default security settings; once relevant restrictions are relaxed, the risks will increase significantly, and you will bear the consequences.","","We recommend using the Lark/Feishu bot integrated with this tool as a private conversational assistant. Do not add it to group chats or allow other users to interact with it, to avoid abuse of permissions or data leakage.","","Please fully understand all usage risks. By using this tool, you are deemed to voluntarily assume all related responsibilities.","","## Star History","","[![Star History Chart](https://api.star-history.com/svg?repos=larksuite/cli\u0026type=Date)](https://star-history.com/#larksuite/cli\u0026Date)","","## Contributing","","Community contributions are welcome! If you find a bug or have feature suggestions, please submit an [Issue](https://github.com/larksuite/cli/issues) or [Pull Request](https://github.com/larksuite/cli/pulls).","","For major changes, we recommend discussing with us first via an Issue.","","Before opening a PR, see [AGENTS.md](./AGENTS.md) for the local build, test, and PR checklist used by contributors and AI agents.","","## License","","This project is licensed under the **MIT License**.","When running, it calls Lark/Feishu Open Platform APIs. <p dir="auto"><a href="https://opensource.org/licenses/MIT" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/fdf2982b9f5d7489dcf44570e714e3a15fce6253e0cc6b5aa61a075aac2ff71b/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f4c6963656e73652d4d49542d79656c6c6f772e737667" alt="License: MIT" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/License-MIT-yellow.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://go.dev/" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b1e207febda59221deaf4c007af2e4de6a9b07a3e81e3d00678de02fb0f5f36f/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f676f2d253345253344312e32332d626c75652e737667" alt="Go Version" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/go-%3E%3D1.23-blue.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/@larksuite/cli" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/8e7d363cda3c71a62a503ec37254f46972f63e8c52c3eb99a478b6a36085b9de/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f6e706d2f762f406c61726b73756974652f636c692e737667" alt="npm version" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/npm/v/@larksuite/cli.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="/larksuite/cli/blob/main/README.zh.md">中文版</a> | <a href="/larksuite/cli/blob/main/README.md">English</a></p>
<p dir="auto">The official <a href="https://www.larksuite.com/" rel="nofollow">Lark/Feishu</a> CLI tool, maintained by the <a href="https://github.com/larksuite">larksuite</a> team — built for humans and AI Agents. Covers core business domains including Messenger, Docs, Base, Sheets, Slides, Calendar, Mail, Tasks, Meetings, Markdown, and more, with 200+ commands and 26 AI Agent <a href="/larksuite/cli/blob/main/skills">Skills</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="#installation--quick-start">Install</a> · <a href="#agent-skills">AI Agent Skills</a> · <a href="#authentication">Auth</a> · <a href="#three-layer-command-system">Commands</a> · <a href="#advanced-usage">Advanced</a> · <a href="#security--risk-warnings-read-before-use">Security</a> · <a href="#contributing">Contributing</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why lark-cli?</h2><a id="user-content-why-lark-cli" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why lark-cli?" href="#why-lark-cli"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Agent-Native Design</strong> — 24 structured <a href="/larksuite/cli/blob/main/skills">Skills</a> out of the box, compatible with popular AI tools — Agents can operate Lark with zero extra setup</li>
<li><strong>Wide Coverage</strong> — 18 business domains, 200+ curated commands, 26 AI Agent <a href="/larksuite/cli/blob/main/skills">Skills</a></li>
<li><strong>AI-Friendly &amp; Optimized</strong> — Every command is tested with real Agents, featuring concise parameters, smart defaults, and structured output to maximize Agent call success rates</li>
<li><strong>Open Source, Zero Barriers</strong> — MIT license, ready to use, just <code>npm install</code></li>
<li><strong>Up and Running in 3 Minutes</strong> — One-click app creation, interactive login, from install to first API call in just 3 steps</li>
<li><strong>Secure &amp; Controllable</strong> — Input injection protection, terminal output sanitization, OS-native keychain credential storage</li>
<li><strong>Three-Layer Architecture</strong> — Shortcuts (human &amp; AI friendly) → API Commands (platform-synced) → Raw API (full coverage), choose the right granularity</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Features</h2><a id="user-content-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Features" href="#features"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation &amp; Quick Start</h2><a id="user-content-installation--quick-start" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation &amp; Quick Start" href="#installation--quick-start"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Requirements</h3><a id="user-content-requirements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Requirements" href="#requirements"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Before you start, make sure you have:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Node.js (<code>npm</code>/<code>npx</code>)</li>
<li>Go <code>v1.23</code>+ and Python 3 (only required for building from source)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quick Start (Human Users)</h3><a id="user-content-quick-start-human-users" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quick Start (Human Users)" href="#quick-start-human-users"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Note for AI assistants:</strong> If you are an AI Agent helping the user with installation, jump directly to <a href="#quick-start-ai-agent">Quick Start (AI Agent)</a>, which contains all the steps you need to complete.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Install</h4><a id="user-content-install" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Install" href="#install"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Choose <strong>one</strong> of the following methods:</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Option 1 — From npm (recommended):</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="npx @larksuite/cli@latest install"><pre>npx @larksuite/cli@latest install</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Option 2 — From source:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Requires Go <code>v1.23</code>+ and Python 3.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="git clone https://github.com/larksuite/cli.git
cd cli
make install

# Install CLI SKILL (required)
npx skills add larksuite/cli -y -g"><pre>git clone https://github.com/larksuite/cli.git
<span class="pl-c1">cd</span> cli
make install

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Install CLI SKILL (required)</span>
npx skills add larksuite/cli -y -g</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Configure &amp; Use</h4><a id="user-content-configure--use" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Configure &amp; Use" href="#configure--use"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# 1. Configure app credentials (one-time, interactive guided setup)
lark-cli config init

# 2. Log in (--recommend auto-selects commonly used scopes)
lark-cli auth login --recommend

# 3. Start using
lark-cli calendar +agenda"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1. Configure app credentials (one-time, interactive guided setup)</span>
lark-cli config init

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2. Log in (--recommend auto-selects commonly used scopes)</span>
lark-cli auth login --recommend

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 3. Start using</span>
lark-cli calendar +agenda</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quick Start (AI Agent)</h2><a id="user-content-quick-start-ai-agent" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quick Start (AI Agent)" href="#quick-start-ai-agent"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">The following steps are for AI Agents. Some steps require the user to complete actions in a browser.</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 1 — Install</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="npx @larksuite/cli@latest install"><pre>npx @larksuite/cli@latest install</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 2 — Configure app credentials</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Run this command in the background. It will output an authorization URL — extract it and send it to the user. The command exits automatically after the user completes the setup in the browser.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="lark-cli config init --new"><pre>lark-cli config init --new</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 3 — Login</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Same as above: run in the background, extract the authorization URL and send it to the user.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="lark-cli auth login --recommend"><pre>lark-cli auth login --recommend</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 4 — Verify</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="lark-cli auth status"><pre>lark-cli auth status</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Agent Skills</h2><a id="user-content-agent-skills" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Agent Skills" href="#agent-skills"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Authentication</h2><a id="user-content-authentication" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Authentication" href="#authentication"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Command</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>auth login</code></td>
<td>OAuth login with interactive selection or CLI flags for scopes</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>auth logout</code></td>
<td>Sign out and remove stored credentials</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>auth status</code></td>
<td>Show current login status and granted scopes</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>auth check</code></td>
<td>Verify a specific scope (exit 0 = ok, 1 = missing)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>auth scopes</code></td>
<td>List all available scopes for the app</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>auth list</code></td>
<td>List all authenticated users</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Interactive login (TUI guides domain and permission level selection)
lark-cli auth login

# Filter by domain
lark-cli auth login --domain calendar,task

# Recommended auto-approval scopes
lark-cli auth login --recommend

# Exact scope
lark-cli auth login --scope &quot;calendar:calendar:read&quot;

# Agent mode: return verification URL immediately, non-blocking
lark-cli auth login --domain calendar --no-wait
# Resume polling later
lark-cli auth login --device-code &lt;DEVICE_CODE&gt;

# Identity switching: execute commands as user or bot
lark-cli calendar +agenda --as user
lark-cli im +messages-send --as bot --chat-id &quot;oc_xxx&quot; --text &quot;Hello&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Interactive login (TUI guides domain and permission level selection)</span>
lark-cli auth login

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Filter by domain</span>
lark-cli auth login --domain calendar,task

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Recommended auto-approval scopes</span>
lark-cli auth login --recommend

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Exact scope</span>
lark-cli auth login --scope <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>calendar:calendar:read<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Agent mode: return verification URL immediately, non-blocking</span>
lark-cli auth login --domain calendar --no-wait
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Resume polling later</span>
lark-cli auth login --device-code <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>DEVICE_CODE<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Identity switching: execute commands as user or bot</span>
lark-cli calendar +agenda --as user
lark-cli im +messages-send --as bot --chat-id <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>oc_xxx<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> --text <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Hello<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Three-Layer Command System</h2><a id="user-content-three-layer-command-system" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Three-Layer Command System" href="#three-layer-command-system"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The CLI provides three levels of granularity, covering everything from quick operations to fully custom API calls:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Shortcuts</h3><a id="user-content-1-shortcuts" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. Shortcuts" href="#1-shortcuts"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Prefixed with <code>+</code>, designed to be friendly for both humans and AI, with smart defaults, table output, and dry-run previews.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="lark-cli calendar +agenda
lark-cli im +messages-send --chat-id &quot;oc_xxx&quot; --text &quot;Hello&quot;
lark-cli docs +create --api-version v2 --doc-format markdown --content $'&lt;title&gt;Weekly Report&lt;/title&gt;\n# Progress\n- Completed feature X'"><pre>lark-cli calendar +agenda
lark-cli im +messages-send --chat-id <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>oc_xxx<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> --text <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Hello<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
lark-cli docs +create --api-version v2 --doc-format markdown --content <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$'</span>&lt;title&gt;Weekly Report&lt;/title&gt;<span class="pl-cce">\n</span># Progress<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>- Completed feature X<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Run <code>lark-cli &lt;service&gt; --help</code> to see all shortcut commands.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. API Commands</h3><a id="user-content-2-api-commands" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. <p dir="auto">Auto-generated from Lark OAPI metadata, curated through evaluation and quality gates — 100+ commands mapped 1:1 to platform endpoints.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="lark-cli calendar calendars list

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">3. Raw API Calls</h3><a id="user-content-3-raw-api-calls" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 3. <p dir="auto">Call any Lark Open Platform endpoint directly, covering 2500+ APIs.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="lark-cli api GET /open-apis/calendar/v4/calendars

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Advanced Usage</h2><a id="user-content-advanced-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Advanced Usage" href="#advanced-usage"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Security &amp; Risk Warnings (Read Before Use)</h2><a id="user-content-security--risk-warnings-read-before-use" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Security &amp; Risk Warnings (Read Before Use)" href="#security--risk-warnings-read-before-use"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This tool can be invoked by AI Agents to automate operations on the Lark/Feishu Open Platform, and carries inherent risks such as model hallucinations, unpredictable execution, and prompt injection. After you authorize Lark/Feishu permissions, the AI Agent will act under your user identity within the authorized scope, which may lead to high-risk consequences such as leakage of sensitive data or unauthorized operations. Please use with caution.</p>
<p dir="auto">To reduce these risks, the tool enables default security protections at multiple layers. However, these risks still exist. We strongly recommend that you do not proactively modify any default security settings; once relevant restrictions are relaxed, the risks will increase significantly, and you will bear the consequences.</p>
<p dir="auto">We recommend using the Lark/Feishu bot integrated with this tool as a private conversational assistant. Do not add it to group chats or allow other users to interact with it, to avoid abuse of permissions or data leakage.</p>
<p dir="auto">Please fully understand all usage risks. By using this tool, you are deemed to voluntarily assume all related responsibilities.</p>
